### [435] [Computing the Exact Pareto Front in Average-Cost Multi-Objective Markov Decision Processes](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.02196)
*Jiping Luo,Nikolaos Pappas*

Main category: eess.SY

Relevance: 15.0

TL;DR: 该论文研究了平均成本多目标马尔可夫决策过程（MOMDP）的帕累托前沿精确表征，发现前沿是位于凸多面体边界上的连续分段线性曲面，每个顶点对应一个确定性策略，相邻顶点仅在一个状态上不同。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有文献主要通过标量化方法近似处理MOMDP的帕累托前沿，或在折扣或简单双目标设置下表征前沿。本文旨在精确表征平均成本MOMDP的完整帕累托前沿，填补这一研究空白。

Method: 通过几何分析证明平均成本MOMDP的帕累托前沿是位于凸多面体边界上的连续分段线性曲面。每个顶点对应一个确定性策略，相邻顶点仅在一个状态上不同。边缘可通过端点策略的凸组合实现，并给出闭式混合系数。

Result: 成功推导出平均成本MOMDP帕累托前沿的精确几何结构，并将其应用于远程状态估计问题，其中前沿的每个顶点对应一个阈值策略。无需显式求解任何MDP即可获得精确帕累托前沿和某些非凸MDP的解。

Conclusion: 本文提供了平均成本MOMDP帕累托前沿的完整几何表征，为多目标强化学习问题提供了新的理论框架和计算工具，特别适用于通信和控制领域的优化问题。

Abstract: Many communication and control problems are cast as multi-objective Markov decision processes (MOMDPs). The complete solution to an MOMDP is the Pareto front. Much of the literature approximates this front via scalarization into single-objective MDPs. Recent work has begun to characterize the full front in discounted or simple bi-objective settings by exploiting its geometry. In this work, we characterize the exact front in average-cost MOMDPs. We show that the front is a continuous, piecewise-linear surface lying on the boundary of a convex polytope. Each vertex corresponds to a deterministic policy, and adjacent vertices differ in exactly one state. Each edge is realized as a convex combination of the policies at its endpoints, with the mixing coefficient given in closed form. We apply these results to a remote state estimation problem, where each vertex on the front corresponds to a threshold policy. The exact Pareto front and solutions to certain non-convex MDPs can be obtained without explicitly solving any MDP.

</details>


### [436] [Best-Arm Identification with Noisy Actuation](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.02255)
*Merve Karakas,Osama Hanna,Lin F. Yang,Christina Fragouli*

Main category: cs.IT

Relevance: 15.0

TL;DR: 研究在多臂老虎机问题中，当臂命令通过离散无记忆信道从中央学习器传输到分布式代理时，如何识别最佳臂，并提出了与信道零错误容量相关的通信方案。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 在分布式学习系统中，中央学习器需要通过通信信道向远程代理发送臂选择命令。当信道存在噪声和容量限制时，如何设计有效的通信方案来确保最佳臂识别是一个重要问题。这结合了多臂老虎机学习和通信理论两个领域。

Method: 根据代理的能力，提出了不同的通信方案。这些方案与底层离散无记忆信道的零错误容量相关，分析了在不同信道条件下如何设计编码和解码策略来传输臂选择命令。

Result: 建立了多臂老虎机问题中臂识别性能与信道零错误容量之间的关系，提出了能够适应不同代理能力的通信方案，并分析了这些方案的理论性能界限。

Conclusion: 该研究将通信理论中的零错误容量概念应用于分布式多臂老虎机学习，为在受限通信条件下设计有效的分布式学习算法提供了理论基础。

Abstract: In this paper, we consider a multi-armed bandit (MAB) instance and study how to identify the best arm when arm commands are conveyed from a central learner to a distributed agent over a discrete memoryless channel (DMC). Depending on the agent capabilities, we provide communication schemes along with their analysis, which interestingly relate to the zero-error capacity of the underlying DMC.

### [437] [Topological Effects in Neural Network Field Theory](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.02313)
*Christian Ferko,James Halverson,Vishnu Jejjala,Brandon Robinson*

Main category: hep-th

Relevance: 15.0

TL;DR: 该论文将神经网络场论扩展到拓扑设置，通过引入离散参数标记拓扑量子数，恢复了BKT相变并验证了玻色弦的T-对偶性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 将神经网络场论扩展到拓扑量子系统，探索神经网络架构如何描述拓扑相变和弦理论中的对偶性。

Method: 扩展神经网络场论构造，引入离散参数标记拓扑量子数，应用于拓扑量子系统和弦理论背景。

Result: 成功恢复了Berezinskii-Kosterlitz-Thouless相变（包括自旋波临界线和高温涡旋增殖），验证了玻色弦的T-对偶性（动量-缠绕交换、Buscher规则、自对偶半径下的流代数增强、非几何T-折叠变换）。

Conclusion: 神经网络场论可以有效地扩展到拓扑设置，为描述拓扑相变和弦理论对偶性提供了新的理论框架。

Abstract: Neural network field theory formulates field theory as a statistical ensemble of fields defined by a network architecture and a density on its parameters. We extend the construction to topological settings via the inclusion of discrete parameters that label the topological quantum number. We recover the Berezinskii--Kosterlitz--Thouless transition, including the spin-wave critical line and the proliferation of vortices at high temperatures. We also verify the T-duality of the bosonic string, showing invariance under the exchange of momentum and winding on $S^1$, the transformation of the sigma model couplings according to the Buscher rules on constant toroidal backgrounds, the enhancement of the current algebra at self-dual radius, and non-geometric T-fold transition functions.

</details>


### [438] [The topological gap at criticality: scaling exponent d + η, universality, and scope](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.01484)
*Matthew Loftus*

Main category: cond-mat.stat-mech

Relevance: 10.0

TL;DR: 该论文提出了一种基于拓扑间隙Δ的有限尺寸标度方法，用于分析自旋模型的临界相关性，并在2D Ising和Potts模型中验证了标度律，但该方法在存在对数修正时失效。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究自旋模型临界相变的拓扑特征，建立拓扑间隙与临界指数之间的关系，为理解相变提供新的拓扑视角。

Method: 使用拓扑间隙Δ（多数自旋α复形的H1总持久性减去密度匹配的零模型）作为序参量，建立有限尺寸标度关系Δ(L,T) = A L^{d+η} G_-(L|t/T_c|)，并在2D Ising、Potts等模型中进行数值验证。

Result: 在2D Ising模型中，α=2.249±0.038与d+η=9/4在0.03σ内一致；2D Potts q=3中α=2.272±0.024与理论值2.267接近。但对于2D Potts q=4（存在对数修正）和原始3D Ising模型，标度律失效，需密度归一化Δ/|M|^{1/2}才能恢复一致性。

Conclusion: 拓扑间隙标度律在代数修正（ω>0）时成立，但在对数修正（ω→0）时失效。该方法为分析临界现象提供了新的拓扑工具，但适用范围有限。

Abstract: The topological gap $Δ= TP_{H_1}^{real} - TP_{H_1}^{shuf}$ -- the excess $H_1$ total persistence of the majority-spin alpha complex over a density-matched null -- encodes critical correlations in spin models. We establish finite-size scaling: $Δ(L,T) = A L^{d+η} G_-(L|t/T_c|)$, with $G_-(x) \sim (1+x/x_0)^{-(1+β/ν)}$. For 2D Ising, $α= 2.249 \pm 0.038$, matching $d+η= 9/4$ to $0.03σ$; the $G_-$ exponent $γ= 1.089 \pm 0.077$ is consistent with $1+β/ν= 9/8$ ($ΔR^2 < 10^{-5}$). For 2D Potts $q=3$ with $L$ up to 1024, $α= 2.272 \pm 0.024$ ($0.2σ$ from $d+η= 2.267$), with two-term corrections to scaling ($R^2 = 0.9999$). The $G_-$ exponent $γ= 1.114$ (68% CI $[1.053, 1.173]$) matches $1+β/ν= 17/15$. Scope boundaries: the law fails for 2D Potts $q=4$ ($α= 2.347 \pm 0.017$, $9.3σ$ from $d+η= 5/2$) where logarithmic corrections prevent convergence, and for raw 3D Ising ($4σ$ from $d+η$), but density normalization $Δ/|M|^{1/2}$ recovers $α= 3.06 \pm 0.04$ ($0.6σ$). The framework fails for first-order, BKT, and percolation. The criterion: $α= d+η$ holds when corrections to scaling are algebraic ($ω> 0$) but fails when logarithmic ($ω\to 0$).

</details>


### [439] [A Determinantal Approach to a Sharp $\ell^1-\ell^\infty-\ell^2$ Norm Inequality](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.01525)
*Jose Antonio Lara Benitez*

Main category: math.CA

Relevance: 5.0

TL;DR: 该论文给出了一个关于向量范数不等式 ‖x‖₁‖x‖∞ ≤ (1+√p)/2 ‖x‖₂² 的简短线性代数证明，并证明了常数 (1+√p)/2 是最优的。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究有限维空间中三种基本范数（ℓ₁、ℓ∞ 和 ℓ₂ 范数）之间的关系，这种不等式在优化和数值分析中有重要应用。

Method: 使用线性代数方法，通过参数化二次型行列式结构来证明不等式。

Result: 成功证明了不等式 ‖x‖₁‖x‖∞ ≤ (1+√p)/2 ‖x‖₂² 对所有 p 维实向量成立，并证明了常数 (1+√p)/2 是最优的。

Conclusion: 该论文提供了一个简洁的线性代数证明，解决了范数不等式问题，并确定了最优常数，对优化和数值分析领域有理论贡献。

Abstract: We give a short linear--algebraic proof of the inequality \[ \|x\|_1\,\|x\|_\infty \le \frac{1+\sqrt{p}}{2}\,\|x\|_2^2, \] valid for every \(x\in\mathbb{R}^p\). This inequality relates three fundamental norms on finite-dimensional spaces and has applications in optimization and numerical analysis. Our proof exploits the determinantal structure of a parametrized family of quadratic forms, and we show the constant $(1+\sqrt{p})/2$ is optimal.

</details>
